# **CDS 2002 Child Interview** **Codebook**

**Number of Variables**

508

```
 Tuesday April 23 2019 3:35 PM

```
```
                    CDS 2002 Child Interview

CHLDREL  "CHILD FILE RELEASE NUMBER 02"            NUM(1.0)

Release Number for Child File

Release 4 Notes: 1) Fixed decimal rounding precision for Q23K1A (n=45); 2) Recoded
incorrect-NA to INAP for records with NA at Q23L3 according to skip logic: Q23L3A-Q23L3D
(n=10); 3) Recoded incorrect-NA to INAP for records with NA at Q23L4 according to skip
logic: Q23L4A1-Q23L4A7 (n=10); Recoded 9999 to 999 for NA to match codebook: Q23L4A1Q23L4A7, Q23L5D, Q23L5K, Q23L6E; 4) Recoded 99 to 9 for NA and 98 to 8 for DK to match
codebook: Q23L9, Q23L10, Q23L34; 5) Added DK codes to codebook: Q23K1A, Q23K21, Q23L3A,
Q23L14C, Q23L30B, Q23L34, Q23L35.

Release 6 Notes: Added coded course and grade values Q23J38A/B/C/F and Q23J39A/B/C/F.

```

```
Code Value/Range Text

Release number 1 - July 2004

Release number 2 - January 2005

Release number 3 - October 2005

Release number 4 - June 2010

Release number 5 - November 2015

Release number 6 - May 2019

```

```

CHLDID01  "2001 INTERVIEW NUMBER"                NUM(5.0)
2001 PSID Main Family Identifier

The values for this variable represent the 2001 interview number of the family in which
this individual was included in 2001

```

```
Code Value/Range Text

Interview number

```

```
Value/Range

   1 - 7,443

```

```

CHLDSN01  "CYPSN 2001"                     NUM(2.0)
2001 PSID Sequence Number

This sequence number variable provides a means of identifying an individual's status with
regard to the family unit at the time of the PSID main family 2001 interview

```

```
Code Value/Range Text

Sequence number of individuals in the PSID family at the
time of the 2001 main family interview
```

```
     1 - 20
```

```
Q23L29   "SEXUAL INTERCOURSE 02"                NUM(1.0)
L29. The next questions are about your sexual experiences. Your responses to the questions
in this section and the other sections are private. The person who interviewed you, your
parents, friends, siblings, teachers, and other people you know will not see your
responses. In fact, the people who will look at your responses will not know your name or
have any way to identify you. Have you ever had sexual intercourse (that is, "had sex",
"made it," etc.)?
Must be 12 years and older for Section L.
Section L was administered by Audio -Computer Assisted Self Interview.

```

```

CDI_02   "CDI Short Form 02"                  NUM(2.0)
Child Depression Inventory 02

This variable is the raw score of the CDI. Items L16a, c, d, f, i were recoded to: 1=0;
2=1; 3=2 and items L16b, e, g, h, j were recoded to: 1=2; 2=1; 3=0. The 10 items were then
summed if valid data points were available on all 10 items.

```

```
Code Value/Range Text

Depression score

Missing score: Child had one or more of the ten items at
L16 missing and thus a score was not computed.

Inap.: if not eligible for ACASI Section L (Age=8-11 yrs
old) or valid response of zero

```

```
Value/Range

     1 - 18

       99

        0

```
